        $ad.css('height', mediaHeight);

        $ad.css('left', mediaPosition.left);

<script>
      if (Drupal.settings.angularmods && Drupal.settings.angularmods.active){
        if (twc.shared && twc.shared.apps) {
          Drupal.settings.angularmods.active.push("shared");
        }
        twc.app = angular.module("twc", Drupal.settings.angularmods.active);

        twc.app.config(["$translateProvider", "twcMessageProvider", "$controllerProvider", "$provide", "$compileProvider", "$filterProvider", function ($translateProvider, twcMessageProvider, $controllerProvider, $provide, $compileProvider, $filterProvider) {
          var locale = (TWC && TWC.Titan && TWC.Titan.locale) || TWC.pco.getNodeValue("user", "locale"), translations = twcMessageProvider.getAll();
          $compileProvider.debugInfoEnabled(window.TWC && TWC.Configs && TWC.Configs.debug === 0 ? false : true);
          if(locale in translations) {
            $translateProvider.translations(locale, translations[locale]);
          }
          $translateProvider.preferredLanguage( locale );

          // setup for dynamic loading.
          var _module = angular.module, apps = Drupal.settings.angularmods.active.concat("twc");
          angular.forEach(apps, function(appName) {
            var app = _module(appName);
            app._controller = app.controller;
            app._service = app.service;
            app._factory = app.factory;
            app._value = app.value;
            app._directive = app.directive;
            // Provider-based controller.
            app.controller = function( name, constructor ) {
                $controllerProvider.register( name, constructor );
                return( this );
            };

            // Provider-based service.
            app.service = function( name, constructor ) {
                $provide.service( name, constructor );
                return( this );
            };

            // Provider-based factory.
            app.factory = function( name, factory ) {
                $provide.factory( name, factory );
                return( this );
            };

            // Provider-based value.
            app.value = function( name, value ) {
                $provide.value( name, value );
                return( this );
            };

            // Provider-based constant.
            app.constant = function( name, value ) {
                $provide.value( name, value );
                return( this );
            };

            // Provider-based filter.
            app.filter = function( name, constructor ) {
                $filterProvider.register( name, constructor );
                return( this );
            };

            // Provider-based directive.
            app.directive = function( name, factory ) {
                $compileProvider.directive( name, factory );
                return( this );
            };
          });

        }]);

        twc.app.run([
          "$rootScope", "$q", "PcoDevice", "twcPco", "$window", "$interpolate", "$sce", function ($rootScope, $q, device, twcPco, $window, $interpolate, $sce) {
            $rootScope.getInternalTrustedUrl = function(url) {
              return $sce.getTrustedResourceUrl(url);
            };
            $rootScope.theme = angular.element("body").hasClass("redcell") ? "redcell" : "reboot";
            $rootScope.isMobile = (Drupal.settings.twc.variant === "little");
            // set touch from window attributes
            $rootScope.isTouch  = ("ontouchstart" in window || (navigator && !!(navigator.msMaxTouchPoints)));
            $q.all(twcPco.get("device").promises).then(function() {
              // set tablet from our device node.
              $rootScope.isTablet = (device.getOpenDDRTablet() === "true");
            });

            if(TWC.pageTitle) {
              var interpolatedPageTitle = $interpolate(TWC.pageTitle);

              $rootScope.$watch(function() {
                return interpolatedPageTitle($rootScope);
              }, function(title) {
                $window.document.title = title;
                $rootScope.pageTitle=title;
              })
            }
            else {
              twclog.error("TWC.pageTitle does not exist");
            }
        }]);
        if (!window.callPhantom) {
          setTimeout(function(){
            angular.bootstrap(document,["twc"], {
              strictDi: true
            });
          },5);
        }
        else {
          // For phantomJS, we need to bootstrap on the browser queue to make the
          // stupid phantom understand that bootstrap is part of the page.
          angular.bootstrap(document,["twc"], {
            strictDi: true
          });
        }
      }
      window.page_bottom_reached = true;
    </script>
</body>
